[Date]      August 1999
[Source]    ViewCS

[Notes]
The package for this model is a sample IBIS template.
It does not contain a device pinout. Add the device pinout to match the
package type and the pinout for the particular design.
These models were extracted from HSPICE models. 
All models are preliminary.
Only driver model data is provided in these models.
Drivers with "slew" in the name have slow slew rate enabled.
Models in this file are simulated as if VCCIO is set to 3.3 V and 2.5 V.

COMMENTS:
All models in TYP, MIN and MAX corners.


TYP =        25C TYP Process, 3.3V and 2.5 V
MAX = (fast) 0C  FF process,  3.6V and 2.7V
MIN = (slow) 85C SS process,  3.0V and 2.3V

Models extracted from SPICE as provided by Altera.

Package is a dummy package with sample drivers.
Actual package pin-outs must be generated by user
according to programmed pin-out.
|
QA using ibis2xtk -pv .00001 -ae .001
|
